.. _8e32bc21-3eb1-413a-902f-d2c9d34a554a:

=======================
Invalid page dictionary
=======================

.. contents::
   :depth: 2

--------------
Classification
--------------

.. list-table::
   :align: center

   * - **Validator**
     - **Validator version**
     - **Error message type**
   * - JHOVE
     - 1.32.1
     - 


.. list-table::
   :align: center

   * - **File format**
     - **Version**
     - **Specification**
     - **Description**
     - **Location**
   * - application/pdf
     - 1.6
     - 
     - 
     - `OPF <https://github.com/openpreserve/format-corpus/corpus/format-corpus/jhove-errors/PDF-HUL-117/me450f12project10_report.pdf>`__

--------
Analyses
--------


------------------
Possible solutions
------------------
.. contents::
   :local:

No suggestion determined. All solutions are listed for browsing :ref:`in here <solutions-list>`.

--------------
